      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-61f86e2ac02d0c0f54d6d5c4"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-55b9baaea1055b4dfc2a"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.148936s; animation-duration: 0.65s;" class="preFade fadeIn"><strong>Privacy Policy</strong></h2><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.159574s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong><br></strong>This privacy policy will explain what information we collect online, why we collect it, and the choices we offer to you.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.170213s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">This privacy policy (Policy) describes the data practices of Vinci Games, Inc. (<strong>Company</strong>), covering its services under its control, including the website known as <em>blacktophoopsvr.com</em>, any and all the Company website, including <em>blacktophoopsvr.com</em>, and any other website or mobile application (collectively "Services"). By using the Services, you are consenting to this Policy and the processing of your data in the manner provided in this Policy. If you do not agree with these terms, please do not use the Services. This Privacy Policy was last updated on<strong> April 15, 2022.&nbsp;</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.180851s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Information we collect<br></strong>We may collect information about the Services you use and how you use them, such as data regarding your usage of the App and activity in the App. We collect PII, DII, and log information about your interactions as described below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.191489s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Personally identifiable information (PII) is information that can be used to identify or contact you online or offline, such as your name, address, email, phone number, photos or audio data, and payment information, or data that is linked to such identifiers. The Services may collect PII when it is provided to us, such as when you use our Services, attempt to contact us, submit a resume or job application, or connect with us on social media or one of our partners.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.202128s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We may also create or collect device-identifiable information (DII), such as cookies, unique device and advertising identifiers, statistical identifiers, usernames, and similar identifiers that are linkable to a browser or device. From these platforms, we may also receive other information, such as your IP address, user agent, timestamps, precise and imprecise geolocation, sensor data, apps, fonts, battery life information, and screen size.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.212766s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Our Services also collect information about your interactions, including navigation paths, search queries, crashes, timestamps, purchases, clicks and shares, and referral URLs. We may combine this data with PII and DII. For efficiencys sake, information about your interactions may be transmitted to our servers while you are not using the Services. We may also partner with third-parties that collect additional information  please see their privacy policies for more details and see below for your choices regarding these parties.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.223404s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong><br><br>Categories and use of PII We Collect</strong>: We have collected the following information from consumers within the past 12 months.&nbsp;We store the personal information we collect as described in this Privacy Policy for as long as you use our Services or as necessary to fulfill the purpose(s) for which it was collected, provide our Services, resolve disputes, establish legal defenses, conduct audits, pursue legitimate business purposes, enforce our agreements, and comply with applicable laws.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.234043s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Examples&nbsp;</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.244681s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">1.Identifiers</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.255319s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Name, email address, IP address, online identifier, images the user uploads, email address, device identifiers, username, or other similar data</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.265957s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">2.&nbsp;Internet or electronic network activity information&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.276596s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Information regarding a consumers interaction with an Internet website, application, or advertisement, in-app activity</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.287234s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">3.Inferences drawn from any information described herein to create a profile about a consumer</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1649253695038_2849"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.297872s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">4. Sensory data</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.308511s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Audio, electronic, visual, or similar information.<br></p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1649253695038_2979"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.319149s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Profile reflects consumer reflecting the consumers preferences, characteristics, psychological trends, preferences, predispositions, behavior, attitudes, intelligence, abilities, and aptitudes.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.329787s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Additional Privacy Rights </strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.340426s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Right to Know.</strong> In relation to your right to access described above, you may request that we disclose to you the categories and specific pieces of personal information that we have collected about you in the preceding 12 months, the categories of sources from which your personal information is collected, the business or commercial purpose for collecting your personal information, the categories of personal information that we disclosed for a business purpose in the preceding 12 months, the categories of third parties with whom we have shared your personal information, and the business or commercial purpose for each disclosure.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.351064s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Right to Delete.</strong> In relation to your right to delete as described above, you may request that we delete any personal information that we have collected from you. Requests should be sent to our email at support@vinci-games.com</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.361702s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>How we use information we collect</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.37234s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We use the information we collect from our Services to provide, maintain, protect and improve our Services, to develop new Services and offerings, and to protect us and our users.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.382979s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">PII is primarily used for business purposes, such as responding to inquiries and providing the Services. When you contact us, we may keep a record of your communication as well as the other information to help solve any issues you might be facing. We may use your email address to inform you about our Services, such as letting you know about changes or improvements. We also use your PII for the following business purposes:&nbsp;</p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.393617s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">To meet the reason for which the PII was provided.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.404255s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">To provide you with information or services you request from us.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.425532s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">To resolve disputes.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.43617s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Preventing potentially fraudulent, prohibited, or illegal activities.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.446809s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Enforcing the Terms of Service.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.457447s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">Performing other duties as required by law.&nbsp;</p></li></ol><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.468085s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We share PII and DII with companies, outside organizations, and individuals for limited reasons and the following business purposes, outlined below:</p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.478723s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We will share PII and other data with companies, outside organizations or individuals if we have your consent to do so.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.489362s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">For external processing - We provide PII to our affiliates or other trusted businesses or persons to process it for us, based on our instructions and in compliance with our Privacy Policy and any other appropriate confidentiality and security measures.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.5s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">For legal reasons - We will share PII with companies, outside organizations or individuals if we have a good-faith belief that access, use, preservation or disclosure of the information is reasonably necessary to meet any applicable law, regulation, legal process or enforceable governmental request, detect, prevent, or otherwise address fraud, security or technical issues or protect against harm to the rights, property or safety of our users or the public as required or permitted by law.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.510638s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">In case of a sale or asset transfer - If we become involved in a merger, acquisition or other transaction involving the sale of some or all of our assets, user information, including PII collected from you through your use of our Services, could be included in the transferred assets. Should such an event occur, we will use reasonable means to notify you, either through email and/or a prominent notice on the Services.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.521277s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We may share aggregated information and DII with our partners such as businesses we have a relationship with advertisers or connected sites. transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.542553s; animation-duration: 0.65s;">We disclose your PII for business purposes to the following categories of third-parties:&nbsp;</p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; We share DII with third-parties primarily for advertising and analytics purposes, for external processing, and for security purposes.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.606383s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><br></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.65s; transition-delay: 0.617021s; animation-duration: 0.65s;"><strong>Third-Parties<br></strong>While we strive to work with reputable companies with good privacy practices, this Policy does not apply to services offered by other companies or individuals, including products or sites that may be displayed to you on the Services. We also do not control the privacy policies and your privacy settings on third-party sites, including social networks. We may use third-parties to help offer you more tailored ads and better Services, such as obtaining analytics about the users of our site and to help tailor advertising to your preferences. Many third-parties participate in self-regulation to offer you a choice regarding receiving targeted ads.             sectionBackground.style.top = '';
          }
